# "You can download English-Indonesian dictionary (323k) that I made. Use WINZIP.EXE to unpack the file. I use dbf file (dBase III+). It has over that 17,000 words. This dictionary is designed to help us (Indonesian) reading English literatures, so I omit simple words that everybody usually knows. You may modify it to meet your needs. It's for free. It's for end user only, not commercial. You can distribute this file to everybody who needs it."
